## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of change of concentration dA/dt as a function of concentration A and time t. In chemical kinetics, rate laws typically follow power-law dependence on concentration (nth-order kinetics), but time-dependent terms may appear in non-autonomous systems such as photolysis, catalytic deactivation, or externally driven reactions.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A (radioactive decay, unimolecular decomposition)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular reaction of same species)
- nth-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate law)
- Mixed-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (second-order with stoichiometric constraint, logistic-like)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (enzyme-catalyzed or saturation kinetics)
- Inhibition kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A**2) (substrate inhibition)
- Autocatalytic reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A)**c2 (autocatalysis with finite reagent)
- Time-dependent first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (reaction with catalyst deactivation or activation)
- Parallel reactions: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (simultaneous first and second order pathways)
- Langmuir-Hinshelwood: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A)**2 (surface-catalyzed reaction kinetics)
- Time-modulated rate: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 + c2 * t) (linearly varying rate constant)
- Fractional order with offset: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 (fractional order with background source/sink)
- Reversible reaction: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (first-order forward and reverse with constant product)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Integer power dependence on concentration → elementary reaction step with molecularity equal to the power (e.g., A**2 for bimolecular)
- Rational functions of concentration (A/(c+A)) → enzyme or surface catalysis with binding/saturation of active sites
- Product of A and (c-A) terms → reversible or autocatalytic reactions with conservation of total mass
- Negative coefficient on leading term → consumption/decay of reactant (net disappearance)
- Explicit time dependence multiplied by concentration → non-autonomous kinetics such as photolysis with varying light or catalyst deactivation
- Sum of different powers of A → parallel competing reaction pathways with different orders
- Denominator with powers of (c+A) → surface-mediated reactions where adsorption competes with reaction
- Square root or fractional power of A (A**0.5) → dissociative adsorption or radical chain mechanisms
- Exponential dependence on t without A → zeroth-order process with time-varying external driving
- Polynomial in A with alternating signs → complex mechanism with both production and consumption terms at different concentration regimes
